Docking SARS-CoV-2

  • All interactions

Note: These results are using theoretical structures of SARS-CoV-2 protein targets, not experimental structures!

This section: We present original results by searching the best current drugs that could be used to treat COVID-19 by using a special set of theoretical targets published by DeepMind team. We calculated the affinity energies for the interactions between all drugs (ligands) available at DrugBank database (DB) and SARS-CoV-2 proteins (targets) obtained with AlphaFold system. These proteins are involved into the virus live cycle.

Hint: Search for a specific drug in the table below or identify it in the dynamic plots to compare it with other drugs. You can export pictures from the plot, zoom in/out, etc. (check the tools by moving the cursor above the plot).

Our Results: The first dynamic plot depicts as a box plot all the interactions of the current drugs with DeepMind targets (SARS-CoV-2 proteins). In addition all the datapoints are plotted to identify each interaction. The current results show that the best drugs for viral proteins nsp2, nsp6, Protein_3a and PLproCterminal could be Phthalocyanine (DB12983), for nsp4 could be R-428 (DB12411) and Phthalocyanine (DB12983), and for M_protein could be Conivaptan (DB00872). Phthalocyanine is under investigation in clinical trial NCT00103246 (Photodynamic Therapy Using Silicon Phthalocyanine 4 in Treating Patients With Actinic Keratosis, Bowen's Disease, Skin Cancer, or Stage I or Stage II Mycosis Fungoides). In addition, in our drug repurposing with experimental structures, we proposed the same Phthalocyanine as a good drug against the ACE2 receptor protein (human). The second dynamic plot presents only the best 50 interactions of the current drugs grouped by DeepMind theoretical targets.

The table shows the best 3421 interactions between all current drugs and DeepMind theoretical structures. Targets=6, Ligands=1600, Ligand families=DeepMind. The compound with the most negative AE value (lowest AE) has the best interaction with a specific target. All the interactions are presented as plots, using AE values for each pair of drug - protein target (blind molecular docking), with a cutoff of -8.5 kcal/mol (only strong interactions).
